paru_many

function paru_demo
%PARU_DEMO: test a single sparse matrix in ParU
%
% Usage: paru_demo
%
% See also paru, paru_make, paru_many, paru_tiny, mldivide.

% ParU, Copyright (c) 2022-2024, Mohsen Aznaveh and Timothy A. Davis,
% All Rights Reserved.
% SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-3.0-or-later

type paru_demo
load west0479
A = west0479 ;
n = size (A,1) ;
b = rand (n,1) ;
x = A\b ;
norm (A*x-b)
[x2,paru_stats] = paru (A,b) ;
paru_stats
norm (A*x2-b)


ans =

   1.2549e-10


paru_stats = 

  struct with fields:

     analysis_time: 3.9697e-04
    factorize_time: 0.0015
        solve_time: 6.5804e-05
          strategy: 'unsymmetric'
